    <script>
      let scanner = null;

      function startQRScanner() {
        const modal = document.getElementById('qrScannerModal');
        const video = document.getElementById('qrScannerVideo');

        modal.classList.remove('hidden');

        // Access camera
        navigator.mediaDevices
          .getUserMedia({ video: { facingMode: 'environment' } })
          .then((stream) => {
            video.srcObject = stream;

            // Initialize QR scanner
            const canvas = document.getElementById('qrScannerCanvas');
            const context = canvas.getContext('2d');

            scanner = setInterval(() => {
              if (video.readyState === video.HAVE_ENOUGH_DATA) {
                canvas.width = video.videoWidth;
                canvas.height = video.videoHeight;
                context.drawImage(video, 0, 0, canvas.width, canvas.height);

                // Use JSQR library for scanning
                const imageData = context.getImageData(0, 0, canvas.width, canvas.height);
                const qrCode = jsQR(imageData.data, imageData.width, imageData.height);

                if (qrCode) {
                  stopQRScanner();
                  const token = qrCode.data.replace('attendance_token:', '');
                  document.getElementById('token').value = token;
                  document.getElementById('token').focus();
                  document.getElementById('token').select();
                  alert('QR code scanned successfully! Token: ' + token);
                }
              }
            }, 100);
          })
          .catch((error) => {
            console.error('Error accessing camera:', error);
            alert('Unable to access camera. Please check permissions.');
            modal.classList.add('hidden');
          });
      }

      function stopQRScanner() {
        const modal = document.getElementById('qrScannerModal');
        const video = document.getElementById('qrScannerVideo');

        modal.classList.add('hidden');

        if (scanner) {
          clearInterval(scanner);
          scanner = null;
        }

        if (video.srcObject) {
          const tracks = video.srcObject.getTracks();
          tracks.forEach((track) => track.stop());
          video.srcObject = null;
        }
      }

      // Close modal on escape key
      document.addEventListener('keydown', (e) => {
        if (e.key === 'Escape') {
          stopQRScanner();
        }
      });

      // Geolocation Logic
      document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => {
        const markForm = document.getElementById('markForm');
        const latInput = document.getElementById('latitude');
        const lngInput = document.getElementById('longitude');
        const statusText = document.querySelector('.animate-pulse');
        const radarPing = document.querySelector('.animate-ping');
        const submitButton = markForm.querySelector('button[type="submit"]');

        // Initially disable submit until location is found
        submitButton.disabled = true;
        submitButton.classList.add('opacity-50', 'cursor-not-allowed');

        if ('geolocation' in navigator) {
          navigator.geolocation.getCurrentPosition(
            (position) => {
              latInput.value = position.coords.latitude.toFixed(6);
              lngInput.value = position.coords.longitude.toFixed(6);

              // Update UI
              statusText.textContent = 'Location Secured';
              statusText.classList.remove('animate-pulse', 'text-gray-500');
              statusText.classList.add('text-green-600', 'font-medium');

              if (radarPing) {
                radarPing.classList.remove('bg-indigo-400');
                radarPing.classList.add('bg-green-400');
              }
              const radarCore = document.querySelector('#gps-radar .bg-indigo-600');
              if (radarCore) {
                radarCore.classList.remove('bg-indigo-600');
                radarCore.classList.add('bg-green-600');
              }

              // Enable form
              submitButton.disabled = false;
              submitButton.classList.remove('opacity-50', 'cursor-not-allowed');
            },
            (error) => {
              console.error('Geolocation error:', error);
              statusText.textContent =
                'Failed to acquire location. Please enable location services.';
              statusText.classList.remove('animate-pulse', 'text-gray-500');
              statusText.classList.add('text-red-500', 'font-medium');

              if (radarPing) {
                radarPing.classList.remove('bg-indigo-400');
                radarPing.classList.add('bg-red-400');
                radarPing.classList.remove('animate-ping');
              }
              const radarCore = document.querySelector('#gps-radar .bg-indigo-600');
              if (radarCore) {
                radarCore.classList.remove('bg-indigo-600');
                radarCore.classList.add('bg-red-600');
              }
            },
            {
              enableHighAccuracy: true,
              timeout: 10000,
              maximumAge: 0,
            }
          );
        } else {
          statusText.textContent = 'Geolocation is not supported by your browser.';
          statusText.classList.remove('animate-pulse', 'text-gray-500');
          statusText.classList.add('text-red-500', 'font-medium');
        }
      });
    </script>

    <!-- Load JSQR & SimpleWebAuthn library -->
    <script src="https://unpkg.com/jsqr@1.4.0/dist/jsQR.js"></script>
    <script src="https://unpkg.com/@simplewebauthn/browser/dist/bundle/index.umd.min.js"></script>

    <script>
      // Intercept the HTMX form submission to enforce Fingerprint verification if enabled
      document.body.addEventListener('htmx:confirm', async function(evt) {
        if (evt.target.id === 'markForm') {
          evt.preventDefault(); // Pause the standard HTMX boost

          const statusText = document.querySelector('.animate-pulse') || document.querySelector('.text-green-600');
          const originalText = statusText.textContent;
          statusText.textContent = 'Verifying Fingerprint...';
          statusText.classList.remove('text-green-600');
          statusText.classList.add('text-indigo-600');

          try {
            const resp = await fetch('/api/webauthn/authenticate/begin/');
            if (!resp.ok) {
              // No credentials registered or server warning. Proceed with standard form.
              evt.detail.issueRequest();
              return;
            }
            
            const options = await resp.json();
            const authResp = await SimpleWebAuthnBrowser.startAuthentication(options);
            
            const verifyResp = await fetch('/api/webauthn/authenticate/complete/', {
              method: 'POST',
              headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
              body: JSON.stringify(authResp)
            });
            
            const verification = await verifyResp.json();
            if (verification.status === 'success') {
              // Successfully verified fingerprint, unlock the request
              evt.detail.issueRequest();
            } else {
              alert("Fingerprint verification failed: " + verification.error);
              statusText.textContent = originalText;
            }
          } catch (err) {
            console.error(err);
            alert("Fingerprint challenge was cancelled.");
            statusText.textContent = originalText;
          }
        }
      });
    </script>

    <div class="mt-6 text-center text-sm text-gray-500">
      <p>Token is case-insensitive</p>
      <p class="mt-1">Contact your lecturer if you don't have a token</p>
    </div>
  </div>
</div>
{% endblock %}

  <script>
    function generateRandomToken() {
      const chars = 'ABCDEFGHIJKLMNOPQRSTUVWXYZ0123456789';
      let token = '';
      for (let i = 0; i < 6; i++) {
        token += chars.charAt(Math.floor(Math.random() * chars.length));
      }
      document.getElementById('token').value = token;
    }

    // Initialize with random token on load and automatically detect location
    window.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => {
      const tokenInput = document.getElementById('token');
      if (tokenInput && !tokenInput.value) {
        generateRandomToken();
      }

      // Automatically get location on page load
      getLocation();

      // Disable form initially until location is verified
      const submitButton = document.querySelector('button[type="submit"]');
      if (submitButton) {
        submitButton.disabled = true;
        submitButton.classList.add('opacity-50', 'cursor-not-allowed');
      }
    });

    // Auto-uppercase token input
    const tokenInput = document.getElementById('token');
    if (tokenInput) {
      tokenInput.addEventListener('input', function (e) {
        this.value = this.value.toUpperCase();
      });
    }

    // Form validation
    const form = document.getElementById('attendanceForm');
    if (form) {
      form.addEventListener('submit', function (e) {
        if (tokenInput && tokenInput.value.length < 4) {
          e.preventDefault();
          tokenInput.focus();
          // Optional: highlight input to show error visually
          tokenInput.classList.add('border-red-500', 'ring-red-500');
          setTimeout(() => tokenInput.classList.remove('border-red-500', 'ring-red-500'), 2000);
        }
      });
    }

    function getLocation() {
      const statusLabel = document.getElementById('locationStatus');
      const latInput = document.getElementById('latitude');
      const lngInput = document.getElementById('longitude');
      const submitButton = document.querySelector('button[type="submit"]');

      if (!navigator.geolocation) {
        statusLabel.textContent =
          'Geolocation is not supported by your browser. Please use a modern browser.';
        statusLabel.classList.add('text-red-500');
        return;
      }

      statusLabel.textContent = 'Locating...';
      statusLabel.classList.remove('text-red-500', 'text-green-600');
      statusLabel.classList.add('text-indigo-600');

      if (submitButton) {
        submitButton.disabled = true;
        submitButton.classList.add('opacity-50', 'cursor-not-allowed');
      }

      navigator.geolocation.getCurrentPosition(
        (position) => {
          latInput.value = position.coords.latitude.toFixed(6);
          lngInput.value = position.coords.longitude.toFixed(6);
          statusLabel.textContent =
            'Location securely captured. Students must be within 50 meters to mark attendance.';
          statusLabel.classList.remove('text-indigo-600');
          statusLabel.classList.add('text-green-600');

          if (submitButton) {
            submitButton.disabled = false;
            submitButton.classList.remove('opacity-50', 'cursor-not-allowed');
          }
        },
        (error) => {
          let errorMsg = 'Unable to retrieve your location';
          if (error.code === error.PERMISSION_DENIED) {
            errorMsg =
              'Location permission denied. Please enable location services to start attendance.';
          } else if (error.code === error.POSITION_UNAVAILABLE) {
            errorMsg = 'Location information unavailable. Please check your GPS.';
          } else if (error.code === error.TIMEOUT) {
            errorMsg = 'Location request timed out. Please try again.';
          }

          statusLabel.textContent = errorMsg;
          statusLabel.classList.remove('text-indigo-600');
          statusLabel.classList.add('text-red-500');

          if (submitButton) {
            submitButton.disabled = true;
            submitButton.classList.add('opacity-50', 'cursor-not-allowed');
          }
        },
        {
          enableHighAccuracy: true,
          timeout: 10000,
          maximumAge: 0,
        }
      );
    }
  </script>
  {% endif %}

  <div
    class="mt-8 rounded-2xl border border-indigo-100 bg-gradient-to-br from-indigo-50 to-blue-50 p-6 shadow-sm md:p-8"
  >
    <div class="flex items-start">
      <div class="flex-shrink-0">
        <div
          class="flex h-10 w-10 items-center justify-center rounded-full bg-indigo-100 text-indigo-600"
        >
          <svg class="h-6 w-6" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 24 24">
            <path
              stroke-linecap="round"
              stroke-linejoin="round"
              stroke-width="2"

            ></path>
          </svg>
        </div>
      </div>
      <div class="ml-4">
        <h3 class="mb-2 text-lg font-bold text-indigo-900">How Attendance Works</h3>

</div>

<script>
  function twoFactorChallenge() {
      const csrfToken = document.querySelector('[name=csrfmiddlewaretoken]')?.value
                      || '{{ csrf_token }}';

      return {
          webauthnSupported: !!window.PublicKeyCredential,
          authenticating: false,
          webauthnDone: false,
          webauthnError: '',

          base64urlToBuffer(base64url) {
              const padding = '='.repeat((4 - base64url.length % 4) % 4);
              const base64 = base64url.replace(/-/g, '+').replace(/_/g, '/') + padding;
              const binary = atob(base64);
              const buffer = new ArrayBuffer(binary.length);
              const view = new Uint8Array(buffer);
              for (let i = 0; i < binary.length; i++) view[i] = binary.charCodeAt(i);
              return buffer;
          },

          bufferToBase64url(buffer) {
              const bytes = new Uint8Array(buffer);
              let binary = '';
              for (let i = 0; i < bytes.length; i++) binary += String.fromCharCode(bytes[i]);
              return btoa(binary).replace(/\+/g, '-').replace(/\//g, '_').replace(/=/g, '');
          },

          async authenticateFingerprint() {
              this.authenticating = true;
              this.webauthnError = '';

              try {
                  // Step 1: Get auth challenge from server
                  const optResp = await fetch('{% url "frontend:webauthn_auth_begin" %}', {
                      method: 'POST',
                      headers: { 'X-CSRFToken': csrfToken },
                  });
                  if (!optResp.ok) {
                      const err = await optResp.json();
                      throw new Error(err.error || 'Failed to get auth options');
                  }
                  const options = await optResp.json();

                  // Step 2: Build publicKey for navigator.credentials.get()
                  const publicKey = {
                      ...options,
                      challenge: this.base64urlToBuffer(options.challenge),
                  };
                  if (options.allowCredentials) {
                      publicKey.allowCredentials = options.allowCredentials.map(c => ({
                          ...c,
                          id: this.base64urlToBuffer(c.id),
                      }));
                  }

                  // Step 3: Prompt biometric
                  const assertion = await navigator.credentials.get({ publicKey });

                  // Step 4: Send assertion to server for verification
                  const body = {
                      id: assertion.id,
                      rawId: this.bufferToBase64url(assertion.rawId),
                      type: assertion.type,
                      response: {
                          clientDataJSON: this.bufferToBase64url(assertion.response.clientDataJSON),
                          authenticatorData: this.bufferToBase64url(assertion.response.authenticatorData),
                          signature: this.bufferToBase64url(assertion.response.signature),
                          userHandle: assertion.response.userHandle
                              ? this.bufferToBase64url(assertion.response.userHandle) : null,
                      },
                  };

                  const verifyResp = await fetch('{% url "frontend:webauthn_auth_complete" %}', {
                      method: 'POST',
                      headers: {
                          'Content-Type': 'application/json',
                          'X-CSRFToken': csrfToken,
                      },
                      body: JSON.stringify(body),
                  });

                  const result = await verifyResp.json();
                  if (!verifyResp.ok || !result.success) {
                      throw new Error(result.error || 'Verification failed');
                  }

                  // Step 5: Submit the attendance form
                  this.webauthnDone = true;
                  setTimeout(() => {
                      document.getElementById('webauthn-submit-form').submit();
                  }, 600);

              } catch (e) {
                  if (e.name === 'NotAllowedError') {
                      this.webauthnError = 'Authentication cancelled or timed out. Try again.';
                  } else {
                      this.webauthnError = e.message || 'Fingerprint verification failed.';
                  }
              } finally {
                  this.authenticating = false;
              }
          },

          init() {
              // Auto-start fingerprint if device supports it and user has credentials
              {% if has_webauthn %}
              if (this.webauthnSupported) {
                  // Small delay so the page renders first
                  setTimeout(() => this.authenticateFingerprint(), 500);
              }
              {% endif %}
          },
      };
  }
</script>
{% endblock %}

    Import student enrollments from a CSV file onto a particular course.
  </p>

<div class="mx-auto max-w-xl">
  {% include 'includes/progress_card.html' %}
  <form method="post" enctype="multipart/form-data" id="upload-form">
    {% csrf_token %}

    <div class="mb-6 rounded-lg border border-gray-200 bg-white p-4 shadow-sm">
      <label
        for="{{ form.course.id_for_label }}"

      <p class="mt-1 text-sm text-red-500">{{ form.course.errors.0 }}</p>

    </div>

    <label
      for="csv-file"
      class="block cursor-pointer rounded-lg border-2 border-dashed border-gray-300 bg-white p-12 text-center transition-colors hover:border-indigo-500"
      id="drop-zone"
    >
      <svg
        class="mx-auto h-12 w-12 text-gray-400"
        fill="none"
        viewBox="0 0 24 24"
        stroke="currentColor"
      >
        <path
          d="M7 16a4 4 0 01-.88-7.903A5 5 0 1115.9 6L16 6a5 5 0 011 9.9M15 13l-3-3m0 0l-3 3m3-3v12"
        />
      </svg>
      <p class="mt-4 text-sm text-gray-600">
        Drag and drop your CSV here, or
        <span class="font-medium text-indigo-600">click to browse</span>
      </p>
      <p class="mt-1 text-xs text-gray-400" id="file-name">No file selected</p>
      <input type="file" name="file" id="csv-file" accept=".csv" class="hidden" />
    </label>

    {% if form.file.errors %}
    <p class="mt-2 text-center text-sm text-red-500">{{ form.file.errors.0 }}</p>
    {% endif %}

    <div class="mt-4 flex items-center justify-between">
      <p class="text-xs text-gray-500">
        Expected columns: <span class="font-medium">Student ID</span> (only the first column is
        read).
      </p>
      <button
        type="submit"
        class="inline-flex items-center rounded-lg bg-indigo-600 px-6 py-2 font-medium text-white transition-colors hover:bg-indigo-700 disabled:cursor-not-allowed disabled:opacity-50"
        id="upload-btn"
        disabled
      >
        <svg class="mr-2 h-4 w-4" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 24 24">
          <path
            stroke-linecap="round"
            stroke-linejoin="round"
            stroke-width="2"
            d="M4 16v1a3 3 0 003 3h10a3 3 0 003-3v-1m-4-8l-4-4m0 0L8 8m4-4v12"
          ></path>
        </svg>
        Upload Enrollments
      </button>
    </div>
  </form>
</div>

<script>
  (function () {
    var fileInput = document.getElementById('csv-file');
    var fileName = document.getElementById('file-name');
    var uploadBtn = document.getElementById('upload-btn');
    var dropZone = document.getElementById('drop-zone');
    var courseSelect = document.querySelector('select[name="course"]');

    // Add Tailwind styles to Django's generated select
    if (courseSelect) {
      courseSelect.classList.add(
        'w-full',
        'rounded-md',
        'border-gray-300',
        'shadow-sm',
        'focus:border-indigo-500',
        'focus:ring-indigo-500'
      );
    }

    function checkFormValidity() {
      if (fileInput.files.length > 0 && courseSelect && courseSelect.value) {
        uploadBtn.disabled = false;
      } else {
        uploadBtn.disabled = true;
      }
    }

    if (courseSelect) {
      courseSelect.addEventListener('change', checkFormValidity);
    }

    fileInput.addEventListener('change', function () {
      if (fileInput.files.length > 0) {
        fileName.textContent = fileInput.files[0].name;
        fileName.classList.add('text-indigo-600', 'font-medium');
        checkFormValidity();
      }
    });

    dropZone.addEventListener('dragover', function (e) {
      e.preventDefault();
      dropZone.classList.add('border-indigo-500', 'bg-indigo-50');
    });
    dropZone.addEventListener('dragleave', function (e) {
      e.preventDefault();
      dropZone.classList.remove('border-indigo-500', 'bg-indigo-50');
    });
    dropZone.addEventListener('drop', function (e) {
      e.preventDefault();
      dropZone.classList.remove('border-indigo-500', 'bg-indigo-50');
      if (e.dataTransfer.files.length > 0) {
        fileInput.files = e.dataTransfer.files;
        fileInput.dispatchEvent(new Event('change'));
      }
    });
  })();
</script>
{% endblock %}

              d="M17.657 16.657L13.414 20.9a1.998 1.998 0 01-2.827 0l-4.244-4.243a8 8 0 1111.314 0z"
            ></path>
            <path
              stroke-linecap="round"
              stroke-linejoin="round"
              stroke-width="2"
              d="M15 11a3 3 0 11-6 0 3 3 0 016 0z"
            ></path>
          </svg>
          <span class="text-lg font-bold">CHECK IN</span>
        </div>
      </button>
    </form>
  </div>

  <div
    class="mt-10 flex items-center space-x-2 rounded-lg border border-green-200 bg-green-50 p-4 text-green-700"
  >
    <span class="relative flex h-3 w-3">
      <span
        class="absolute inline-flex h-full w-full animate-ping rounded-full bg-green-400 opacity-75"
      ></span>
      <span class="relative inline-flex h-3 w-3 rounded-full bg-green-500"></span>
    </span>
    <span class="text-sm font-medium" id="gps-status">GPS Signal: Strong (Accuracy: 5m)</span>
  </div>

  <!-- Map showing student location and geofence -->
  <div class="mt-8 w-full max-w-md">
    <h3 class="mb-4 text-center text-lg font-semibold text-gray-900 dark:text-white">
      Your Location
    </h3>
    <div id="map" class="z-0 h-64 w-full rounded-lg shadow-md"></div>
  </div>
</div>

<script src="https://unpkg.com/@zxing/library@latest"></script>
<script>
  // QR Code Scanner Functionality
  const scanQrBtn = document.getElementById('scan-qr-btn');
  const qrScanner = document.getElementById('qr-scanner');
  const video = document.getElementById('video');
  const canvas = document.getElementById('canvas');
  const tokenInput = document.getElementById('attendance-token');
  const form = document.getElementById('attendance-form');

  let codeReader;
  let scanning = false;

  scanQrBtn.addEventListener('click', async () => {
    if (scanning) {
      // Stop scanning
      scanning = false;
      qrScanner.classList.add('hidden');
      scanQrBtn.textContent = 'Scan QR Code';
      if (codeReader) {
        codeReader.reset();
      }
    } else {
      // Start scanning
      try {
        codeReader = new ZXing.BrowserQRCodeReader();
        const result = await codeReader.decodeFromVideoElement(video, (result, err) => {
          if (result) {
            const token = result.text.replace('attendance_token:', '');
            tokenInput.value = token;
            scanning = false;
            qrScanner.classList.add('hidden');
            scanQrBtn.textContent = 'Scan QR Code';
            if (codeReader) {
              codeReader.reset();
            }
            // Auto-submit form
            form.submit();
          }
        });
        qrScanner.classList.remove('hidden');
        scanQrBtn.textContent = 'Stop Scanning';
        scanning = true;
      } catch (error) {
        console.error('QR Scanner Error:', error);
        alert('Unable to access camera. Please check permissions.');
      }
    }
  });

  // Form submission
  form.addEventListener('submit', (e) => {
    e.preventDefault();
    const token = tokenInput.value.trim();

    if (!token) {
      alert('Please enter an attendance token or scan a QR code');
      return;
    }

    const btnText = document.querySelector('button span.font-bold');
    btnText.innerText = 'LOCATING...';

    // Get current location
    if (navigator.geolocation) {
      navigator.geolocation.getCurrentPosition(
        (position) => {
          // Submit form with location data
          const formData = new FormData(form);
          formData.append('latitude', position.coords.latitude);
          formData.append('longitude', position.coords.longitude);
          formData.append('attendance_token', formData.get('token'));

          fetch('{% url "submit_location" %}', {
            method: 'POST',
            headers: {
              'X-CSRFToken': formData.get('csrfmiddlewaretoken'),
              Accept: 'application/json',
            },
            body: formData,
          })
            .then((response) => response.json())
            .then((data) => {
              if (data.status === 'Attendance marked successfully') {
                btnText.innerText = 'SUCCESS!';
                setTimeout(() => {
                  btnText.innerText = 'CHECK IN';
                  tokenInput.value = '';
                }, 2000);
              } else {
                alert(data.error || 'Failed to mark attendance');
                btnText.innerText = 'CHECK IN';
              }
            })
            .catch((error) => {
              console.error('Error:', error);
              alert('Network error. Please try again.');
              btnText.innerText = 'CHECK IN';
            });
        },
        (error) => {
          console.error('Geolocation Error:', error);
          alert('Unable to get location. Please enable GPS.');
          btnText.innerText = 'CHECK IN';
        }
      );
    } else {
      alert('Geolocation not supported');
      btnText.innerText = 'CHECK IN';
    }
  });

  // Initialize Map - center on student's location once acquired
  var defaultLat = 5.6037,
    defaultLng = -0.187;
  var map = L.map('map').setView([defaultLat, defaultLng], 17);

  // Add OpenStreetMap Tiles
  L.tileLayer('https://tile.openstreetmap.org/{z}/{x}/{y}.png', {
    maxZoom: 19,
    attribution: 'Â© OpenStreetMap',
  }).addTo(map);

  // Show the Student's Location (Blue Dot) and center map on it
  if (navigator.geolocation) {
    navigator.geolocation.getCurrentPosition(
      function (position) {
        var lat = position.coords.latitude;
        var lng = position.coords.longitude;

        // Update the GPS signal indicator
        document.querySelector('#gps-status').textContent =
          'GPS Signal: Strong (Accuracy: ' + Math.round(position.coords.accuracy) + 'm)';

        map.setView([lat, lng], 17);

        L.marker([lat, lng]).addTo(map).bindPopup('You are here').openPopup();
      },
      function (error) {
        console.log('Geolocation error: ' + error.message);
        document.querySelector('#gps-status').textContent =
          'GPS Signal: Unavailable - ' + error.message;
      },
      { enableHighAccuracy: true, timeout: 10000, maximumAge: 0 }
    );
  }
</script>

{% endblock %}

  <body class="bg-gradient-to-br from-indigo-50 to-blue-50 dark:from-gray-900 dark:to-gray-800">

      <!-- Logo and Brand -->

    <script>
      document.body.addEventListener('htmx:configRequest', (event) => {
        event.detail.headers['X-CSRFToken'] = '{{ csrf_token }}';
      });

      // Show/hide conditional fields based on role
      document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function () {
        const roleLecturer = document.getElementById('role-lecturer');
        const roleStudent = document.getElementById('role-student');
        const lecturerFields = document.getElementById('lecturer-fields');
        const studentFields = document.getElementById('student-fields');

        function toggleFields() {
          if (roleLecturer.checked) {
            lecturerFields.classList.remove('hidden');
            studentFields.classList.add('hidden');
          } else if (roleStudent.checked) {
            studentFields.classList.remove('hidden');
            lecturerFields.classList.add('hidden');
          }
        }

        roleLecturer.addEventListener('change', toggleFields);
        roleStudent.addEventListener('change', toggleFields);

        // Initial toggle
        toggleFields();
      });
    </script>
  </body>
</html>

FILE: templates/includes/progress_card.html
================================================
{% if task_id %}
<div id="progress-card" class="card shadow-sm mb-4 border-0" style="background: linear-gradient(135deg, #667eea22, #764ba222); border-radius: 12px;">
  <div class="card-body p-4">
    <div class="d-flex align-items-center mb-3">
      <div id="progress-spinner" class="spinner-border spinner-border-sm text-primary me-2" role="status"></div>
      <h6 class="mb-0 fw-bold" id="progress-title">Processing Upload...</h6>
    </div>
    <p class="text-muted small mb-2" id="progress-status">Starting...</p>
    <div class="progress mb-2" style="height: 8px; border-radius: 4px; background: #e9ecef;">
      <div id="progress-bar" class="progress-bar progress-bar-striped progress-bar-animated" role="progressbar" style="width: 0%; border-radius: 4px; background: linear-gradient(90deg, #667eea, #764ba2);"></div>
    </div>
    <small class="text-muted" id="progress-count"></small>
    <!-- Result area (hidden until complete) -->
    <div id="progress-result" class="mt-3" style="display:none;"></div>
  </div>
</div>

<script>
(function() {
  const taskId = '{{ task_id }}';
  const statusUrl = '{% url "frontend:task_status" task_id %}';
  const bar = document.getElementById('progress-bar');
  const statusEl = document.getElementById('progress-status');
  const countEl = document.getElementById('progress-count');
  const titleEl = document.getElementById('progress-title');
  const spinner = document.getElementById('progress-spinner');
  const resultEl = document.getElementById('progress-result');
  let pollInterval;

  function poll() {
    fetch(statusUrl)
      .then(r => r.json())
      .then(data => {
        if (data.state === 'PROGRESS') {
          const pct = Math.round((data.current / data.total) * 100);
          bar.style.width = pct + '%';
          bar.setAttribute('aria-valuenow', pct);
          statusEl.textContent = data.status || 'Processing...';
          countEl.textContent = data.current + ' / ' + data.total;
        } else if (data.state === 'SUCCESS') {
          clearInterval(pollInterval);
          bar.style.width = '100%';
          bar.classList.remove('progress-bar-animated', 'progress-bar-striped');
          bar.style.background = '#10b981';
          spinner.style.display = 'none';
          titleEl.innerHTML = '<i class="fas fa-check-circle text-success me-1"></i> Upload Complete';
          statusEl.textContent = 'All records have been processed.';
          countEl.textContent = '';

          // Show structured result
          const r = data.result || {};
          let html = '<div class="alert alert-success py-2 px-3 mb-0 small">';
          if (r.created !== undefined) html += '<strong>' + r.created + '</strong> created';
          if (r.enrolled !== undefined) html += '<strong>' + r.enrolled + '</strong> enrolled';
          if (r.skipped !== undefined) html += ', <strong>' + r.skipped + '</strong> skipped';
          if (r.total !== undefined) html += ' (of ' + r.total + ' total)';
          if (r.course) html += ' in <strong>' + r.course + '</strong>';
          html += '</div>';
          resultEl.innerHTML = html;
          resultEl.style.display = 'block';
        } else if (data.state === 'FAILURE') {
          clearInterval(pollInterval);
          bar.style.width = '100%';
          bar.classList.remove('progress-bar-animated', 'progress-bar-striped');
          bar.style.background = '#ef4444';
          spinner.style.display = 'none';
          titleEl.innerHTML = '<i class="fas fa-exclamation-circle text-danger me-1"></i> Upload Failed';
          statusEl.textContent = data.error || 'An error occurred during processing.';
          countEl.textContent = '';
        }
        // PENDING â€” task hasn't started yet, keep waiting
      })
      .catch(() => {
        statusEl.textContent = 'Checking status...';
      });
  }

  poll();
  pollInterval = setInterval(poll, 1500);
})();
</script>
{% endif %}

FILE: templates/partials/pagination.html
================================================
{% if page_obj.has_other_pages %}
<nav
  class="mt-4 flex items-center justify-between rounded-lg border-t border-gray-200 bg-white px-4 py-3 shadow sm:px-6"
  aria-label="Pagination"
>
  <div class="hidden sm:block">
    <p class="text-sm text-gray-700">
      Showing <span class="font-medium">{{ page_obj.start_index }}</span> to
      <span class="font-medium">{{ page_obj.end_index }}</span> of
      <span class="font-medium">{{ page_obj.paginator.count }}</span> results
    </p>
  </div>
  <div class="flex flex-1 justify-between gap-1 sm:justify-end">
    {% if page_obj.has_previous %}
    <a
      href="?{% for key, value in request.GET.items %}{% if key != 'page' %}{{ key }}={{ value }}&{% endif %}{% endfor %}page={{ page_obj.previous_page_number }}"
      class="relative inline-flex items-center rounded-md bg-white px-3 py-2 text-sm font-semibold text-gray-900 ring-1 ring-inset ring-gray-300 hover:bg-gray-50"
    >
      <svg class="mr-1 h-4 w-4" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 24 24">
        <path
          stroke-linecap="round"
          stroke-linejoin="round"
          stroke-width="2"
          d="M15 19l-7-7 7-7"
        ></path>
      </svg>
      Previous
    </a>
    {% endif %} {% for num in page_obj.paginator.page_range %} {% if page_obj.number == num %}
    <span
      class="relative hidden items-center rounded-md bg-indigo-600 px-4 py-2 text-sm font-semibold text-white sm:inline-flex"
      >{{ num }}</span
    >
    {% elif num > page_obj.number|add:"-3" and num < page_obj.number|add:"3" %}
    <a
      href="?{% for key, value in request.GET.items %}{% if key != 'page' %}{{ key }}={{ value }}&{% endif %}{% endfor %}page={{ num }}"
      class="relative hidden items-center rounded-md px-4 py-2 text-sm font-semibold text-gray-900 ring-1 ring-inset ring-gray-300 hover:bg-gray-50 sm:inline-flex"
      >{{ num }}</a
    >
    {% elif num == 1 or num == page_obj.paginator.num_pages %}
    <a
      href="?{% for key, value in request.GET.items %}{% if key != 'page' %}{{ key }}={{ value }}&{% endif %}{% endfor %}page={{ num }}"
      class="relative hidden items-center rounded-md px-4 py-2 text-sm font-semibold text-gray-900 ring-1 ring-inset ring-gray-300 hover:bg-gray-50 sm:inline-flex"
      >{{ num }}</a
    >
    {% elif num == 2 or num == page_obj.paginator.num_pages|add:"-1" %}
    <span class="relative hidden items-center px-2 py-2 text-sm text-gray-500 sm:inline-flex"
      >&hellip;</span
    >
    {% endif %} {% endfor %} {% if page_obj.has_next %}
    <a
      href="?{% for key, value in request.GET.items %}{% if key != 'page' %}{{ key }}={{ value }}&{% endif %}{% endfor %}page={{ page_obj.next_page_number }}"
      class="relative inline-flex items-center rounded-md bg-white px-3 py-2 text-sm font-semibold text-gray-900 ring-1 ring-inset ring-gray-300 hover:bg-gray-50"
    >
      Next
      <svg class="ml-1 h-4 w-4" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 24 24">
        <path
          stroke-linecap="round"
          stroke-linejoin="round"
          stroke-width="2"
          d="M9 5l7 7-7 7"
        ></path>
      </svg>
    </a>
    {% endif %}
  </div>
</nav>
{% endif %}

<script>
  (function() {
      const canvas = document.getElementById('weeklyChart');
      if (!canvas) return;
      
      const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');
      const labels = {{ week_labels|safe }};
      const data = {{ week_counts|safe }};

      // Destroy previous instances to prevent Canvas duplication errors under HTMX SPA
      if (window.weeklyTrendChart) {
          window.weeklyTrendChart.destroy();
      }

      window.weeklyTrendChart = new Chart(ctx, {
          type: 'bar',
          data: {
              labels: labels,
              datasets: [{
                  label: 'Sessions',
                  data: data,
                  backgroundColor: 'rgba(99, 102, 241, 0.7)',
                  borderColor: 'rgb(99, 102, 241)',
                  borderWidth: 1,
                  borderRadius: 6,
                  hoverBackgroundColor: 'rgba(99, 102, 241, 0.9)',
              }]
          },
          options: {
              responsive: true,
              maintainAspectRatio: false,
              plugins: {
                  legend: { display: false },
                  tooltip: {
                      backgroundColor: '#1f2937',
                      titleFont: { size: 13 },
                      bodyFont: { size: 12 },
                      padding: 10,
                      cornerRadius: 8,
                  }
              },
              scales: {
                  y: {
                      beginAtZero: true,
                      ticks: {
                          stepSize: 1,
                          font: { size: 12 },
                          color: '#6b7280'
                      },
                      grid: { color: '#f3f4f6' }
                  },
                  x: {
                      ticks: {
                          font: { size: 11 },
                          color: '#6b7280'
                      },
                      grid: { display: false }
                  }
              }
          }
      });
  })();
</script>

      <button id="register-biometrics" class="w-full flex justify-center items-center gap-2 rounded-lg bg-indigo-50 px-4 py-2.5 text-sm font-medium text-indigo-700 hover:bg-indigo-100 transition-colors">
        <svg class="w-5 h-5" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" stroke-width="2" d="M12 11c0 3.517-1.009 6.799-2.753 9.571m-3.44-2.04l.054-.09A13.916 13.916 0 008 11a4 4 0 118 0c0 1.017-.07 2.019-.203 3m-2.118 6.844A21.88 21.88 0 0015.171 17m3.839 1.132c.645-2.266.99-4.659.99-7.132A8 8 0 008 4.07M3 15.364c.64-1.319 1-2.8 1-4.364 0-1.457.39-2.823 1.07-4"></path></svg>

  <script src="https://unpkg.com/@simplewebauthn/browser/dist/bundle/index.umd.min.js"></script>
  <script>
    document.getElementById('register-biometrics').addEventListener('click', async () => {
        const msg = document.getElementById('bio-msg');
        msg.className = 'text-xs font-medium mt-3 text-center text-indigo-600 block';
        msg.innerText = 'Requesting device biometrics...';
        try {
            const resp = await fetch('/api/webauthn/register/begin/');
            const options = await resp.json();
            
            const authResp = await SimpleWebAuthnBrowser.startRegistration(options);
            
            const verifyResp = await fetch('/api/webauthn/register/complete/', {
                method: 'POST',
                headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
                body: JSON.stringify(authResp)
            });
            
            const verification = await verifyResp.json();
            if (verification.status === 'success') {
                msg.className = 'text-xs font-medium mt-3 text-center text-green-600 block';
                msg.innerText = 'Biometrics successfully registered! âœ“';
            } else {
                msg.className = 'text-xs font-medium mt-3 text-center text-red-600 block';
                msg.innerText = verification.error || 'Failed to register.';
            }
        } catch (err) {
            console.error(err);
            msg.className = 'text-xs font-medium mt-3 text-center text-red-600 block';
            msg.innerText = 'Registration cancelled or failed.';
        }
    });
  </script>

  <div class="rounded-lg bg-white p-6 shadow lg:col-span-2">
    <h2 class="mb-4 text-lg font-semibold text-gray-900">
      Enrolled Courses ({{ enrollments.count }})
    </h2>
    {% if enrollments %}
    <div class="space-y-3">
      {% for enrollment in enrollments %}

        href="{% url 'frontend:course_detail' enrollment.course.id %}"
        class="block rounded-lg border border-gray-200 p-4 transition hover:border-green-300 hover:bg-green-50"
      >
        <div class="flex items-center justify-between">
          <div>
            <p class="font-medium text-gray-900">{{ enrollment.course.name }}</p>
            <p class="text-sm text-gray-500">{{ enrollment.course.course_code }}</p>
          </div>
          <span class="text-xs text-gray-500"
            >Enrolled: {{ enrollment.enrolled_at|date:"M d, Y" }}</span
          >
        </div>
      </a>
      {% endfor %}
    </div>

            @keyup.enter="verifyOtp()"

  <h3 class="mb-3 text-lg font-semibold text-gray-900 dark:text-white">2FA Status</h3>

      >

        credentials.count|pluralize }}){% else %}Not configured{% endif %}
      </span>
    </div>
    <div
      class="{% if has_otp %}bg-green-50 dark:bg-green-900/20{% else %}bg-gray-50 dark:bg-gray-700{% endif %} flex items-center rounded-lg p-3"
    >
      <span
        class="{% if has_otp %}bg-green-500{% else %}bg-gray-300{% endif %} mr-3 h-3 w-3 rounded-full"
      ></span>
      <span
        class="{% if has_otp %}text-green-800 dark:text-green-300{% else %}text-gray-500 dark:text-gray-400{% endif %} text-sm"
      >
        OTP: {% if has_otp %}Active{% else %}Not configured{% endif %}
      </span>
    </div>
  </div>
  {% if not has_webauthn and not has_otp %}
  <p class="mt-3 text-sm text-yellow-600 dark:text-yellow-400">
    You have no 2FA method configured. If a lecturer enables 2FA for attendance, you will be
    redirected here to set it up.
  </p>
  {% endif %}
</div>

<script>
  function twoFactorSetup() {
    const csrfToken =
      document.querySelector('[name=csrfmiddlewaretoken]')?.value || '{{ csrf_token }}';

    return {
      // WebAuthn state
      webauthnSupported: !!window.PublicKeyCredential,
      registering: false,
      webauthnMsg: '',
      webauthnOk: false,

      // OTP state
      otpSetupStarted: false,
      otpLoading: false,
      otpQrSvg: '',
      otpSecret: '',
      otpCode: '',
      otpVerifying: false,
      otpMsg: '',
      otpOk: false,

      // ========== Base64url helpers ==========
      base64urlToBuffer(base64url) {
        const padding = '='.repeat((4 - (base64url.length % 4)) % 4);
        const base64 = base64url.replace(/-/g, '+').replace(/_/g, '/') + padding;
        const binary = atob(base64);
        const buffer = new ArrayBuffer(binary.length);
        const view = new Uint8Array(buffer);
        for (let i = 0; i < binary.length; i++) {
          view[i] = binary.charCodeAt(i);
        }
        return buffer;
      },

      bufferToBase64url(buffer) {
        const bytes = new Uint8Array(buffer);
        let binary = '';
        for (let i = 0; i < bytes.length; i++) {
          binary += String.fromCharCode(bytes[i]);
        }
        return btoa(binary).replace(/\+/g, '-').replace(/\//g, '_').replace(/=/g, '');
      },

      // ========== Fingerprint Registration ==========
      async registerFingerprint() {
        this.registering = true;
        this.webauthnMsg = '';

        try {
          // Step 1: Get registration options from server
          const optionsResp = await fetch('{% url "frontend:webauthn_register_begin" %}', {
            method: 'POST',
            headers: { 'X-CSRFToken': csrfToken },
          });
          if (!optionsResp.ok) {
            const err = await optionsResp.json();
            throw new Error(err.error || 'Failed to get registration options');
          }
          const options = await optionsResp.json();

          // Step 2: Convert base64url fields to ArrayBuffer for WebAuthn API
          const publicKey = {
            ...options,
            challenge: this.base64urlToBuffer(options.challenge),
            user: {
              ...options.user,
              id: this.base64urlToBuffer(options.user.id),
            },
          };
          if (options.excludeCredentials) {
            publicKey.excludeCredentials = options.excludeCredentials.map((c) => ({
              ...c,
              id: this.base64urlToBuffer(c.id),
            }));
          }

          // Step 3: Prompt user for biometric
          const credential = await navigator.credentials.create({ publicKey });

          // Step 4: Send response to server
          const body = {
            id: credential.id,
            rawId: this.bufferToBase64url(credential.rawId),
            type: credential.type,
            response: {
              clientDataJSON: this.bufferToBase64url(credential.response.clientDataJSON),
              attestationObject: this.bufferToBase64url(credential.response.attestationObject),
            },
          };

          const verifyResp = await fetch('{% url "frontend:webauthn_register_complete" %}', {
            method: 'POST',
            headers: {
              'Content-Type': 'application/json',
              'X-CSRFToken': csrfToken,
            },
            body: JSON.stringify(body),
          });

          const result = await verifyResp.json();
          if (verifyResp.ok && result.success) {
            this.webauthnMsg = result.message || 'Fingerprint registered!';
            this.webauthnOk = true;
            setTimeout(() => location.reload(), 1200);
          } else {
            throw new Error(result.error || 'Registration failed');
          }
        } catch (e) {
          if (e.name === 'NotAllowedError') {
            this.webauthnMsg = 'Authentication was cancelled or timed out.';
          } else if (e.name === 'InvalidStateError') {
            this.webauthnMsg = 'This credential is already registered.';
          } else {
            this.webauthnMsg = e.message || 'Registration failed. Please try again.';
          }
          this.webauthnOk = false;
        } finally {
          this.registering = false;
        }
      },

      // ========== OTP Setup ==========
      async beginOtpSetup() {
        this.otpLoading = true;
        this.otpMsg = '';

        try {
          const resp = await fetch('{% url "frontend:student_setup_otp" %}', {
            method: 'POST',
            headers: { 'X-CSRFToken': csrfToken },
          });
          if (!resp.ok) {
            const err = await resp.json();
            throw new Error(err.error || 'Failed to generate OTP');
          }
          const data = await resp.json();
          this.otpQrSvg = data.qr_svg;
          this.otpSecret = data.secret;
          this.otpSetupStarted = true;
        } catch (e) {
          this.otpMsg = e.message || 'Failed to set up OTP.';
          this.otpOk = false;
        } finally {
          this.otpLoading = false;
        }
      },

      async verifyOtp() {
        if (this.otpCode.length !== 6) return;
        this.otpVerifying = true;
        this.otpMsg = '';

        try {
          const formData = new FormData();
          formData.append('otp_code', this.otpCode);

          const resp = await fetch('{% url "frontend:student_verify_otp" %}', {
            method: 'POST',
            headers: { 'X-CSRFToken': csrfToken },
            body: formData,
          });
          const data = await resp.json();
          if (resp.ok && data.success) {
            this.otpMsg = data.message || 'OTP enabled!';
            this.otpOk = true;
            setTimeout(() => location.reload(), 1200);
          } else {
            throw new Error(data.error || 'Verification failed');
          }
        } catch (e) {
          this.otpMsg = e.message || 'Invalid code.';
          this.otpOk = false;
        } finally {
          this.otpVerifying = false;
        }
      },
    };
  }
</script>
{% endblock %}

================================================
{% extends 'base.html' %} {% block title %}Upload Students - Exodus{% endblock %} {% block content %}
<div class="mb-6">

<script>
  (function () {
    var fileInput = document.getElementById('csv-file');
    var fileName = document.getElementById('file-name');
    var uploadBtn = document.getElementById('upload-btn');
    var dropZone = document.getElementById('drop-zone');

    fileInput.addEventListener('change', function () {
      if (fileInput.files.length > 0) {
        fileName.textContent = fileInput.files[0].name;
        fileName.classList.add('text-indigo-600', 'font-medium');
        uploadBtn.disabled = false;
      }
    });

    dropZone.addEventListener('dragover', function (e) {
      e.preventDefault();
      dropZone.classList.add('border-indigo-500', 'bg-indigo-50');
    });
    dropZone.addEventListener('dragleave', function (e) {
      e.preventDefault();
      dropZone.classList.remove('border-indigo-500', 'bg-indigo-50');
    });
    dropZone.addEventListener('drop', function (e) {
      e.preventDefault();
      dropZone.classList.remove('border-indigo-500', 'bg-indigo-50');
      if (e.dataTransfer.files.length > 0) {
        fileInput.files = e.dataTransfer.files;
        fileInput.dispatchEvent(new Event('change'));
      }
    });
  })();
</script>
{% endblock %}



================================================
FILE: .github/workflows/ci.yml
================================================
name: CI

on:
  push:
    branches: [main]
  pull_request:
    branches: [main]

jobs:
  test:
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest

    services:
      redis:
        image: redis:7-alpine
        ports:
          - 6379:6379

    env:
      DJANGO_SETTINGS_MODULE: attendance_system.settings
      DJANGO_SECRET_KEY: ci-test-secret-key-at-least-32-bytes-for-jwt-compliance
      DJANGO_DEBUG: "True"

    steps:
      - uses: actions/checkout@v4

      - name: Set up Python 3.12
        uses: actions/setup-python@v5
        with:
          python-version: "3.12"
          cache: pip

      - name: Set up Node.js 20
        uses: actions/setup-node@v4
        with:
          node-version: "20"
          cache: npm

      - name: Install Python dependencies
        run: |
          python -m pip install --upgrade pip
          pip install -r requirements.txt

      - name: Install Node dependencies & build assets
        run: |
          npm ci
          npm run build

      - name: Run Django system checks
        run: python manage.py check

      - name: Run tests with coverage
        run: |
          coverage run manage.py test --verbosity=2
          coverage report --fail-under=50
          
      - name: Run deploy check (audit)
        run: python manage.py check --deploy 2>&1 || true
